It is mathematically impossible to OOM crash.\n15: - **Asynchronous Task Queue**: Upload 1,000 images at once—the built-in SQLite queue worker will flawlessly process them sequentially while serving real-time queue position UI updates to the frontend.\n16: - **Stunning UI**: A sleek, dark-mode Next.js interface featuring glassmorphism, Framer Motion queue animations, and a satisfying Before/After image comparison slider.\n17: \n18: ## 🚀 Architecture\n19: \n20: The application is split into two Dockerized microservices:\n21: \n22: 1. **Frontend (`web/`)**: Next.js 14, TailwindCSS, Framer Motion. Polling-based progress tracking.\n23: 2. **Backend (`api/`)**: FastAPI, SQLite, and Python ThreadPoolExecutors. Heavy AI inferences are dispatched to isolated micro-worker scripts (`gfpgan_worker.py`, `realesrgan_worker.py`).\n24: \n25: ## 🛠️ Quick Start (Docker)\n26: \n27: Ensure you have Docker and Docker Compose installed.\n28: \n29: ```bash\n30: git clone https://github.com/BhavyaKansal20/ChromaCrystal_UHD.git\n31: cd ChromaCrystal_UHD\n32: docker compose up --build -d\n33: ```\n34: \n35: Access the web interface at `http://localhost:3000`.\n36: \n37: ## 🧠 Memory Isolation Design\n38: \n39: Running multiple Heavy PyTorch models simultaneously traditionally causes a `SIGKILL 137` (Out of Memory) crash in limited Docker environments. \n40: ChromaCrystal solves this by:\n41: 1. **Queuing**: Only one image enters the pipeline at a time.\n42: 2. **Subprocess Delegation**: Instead of loading GFPGAN and ESRGAN into the main FastAPI memory, they are instantiated inside temporary subprocesses.\n43: 3. **Instant Reclamation**: The moment the upscaler finishes, the subprocess terminates, instantly handing 100% of the memory back to the host machine before the next model is loaded.\n44: \n45: ## 📦 Dependencies\n46: \n47: - **FastAPI** & **Uvicorn**\n48: - **PyTorch**, **Torchvision**\n49: - **OpenCV**\n50: - **DeOldify**, **GFPGAN**, **Real-ESRGAN**\n51: - **Next.js**, **React**, **TailwindCSS**\n52: \n53: ## 🤝 Contributing\n54: Feel free to open issues and submit Pull Requests! \n55: \n56: ---\n57: *Built with ❤️ for restoring history.*\n58: \nThe above content shows the entire, complete file contents of the requested file.\n"}
